\"text\": \"The Envoy Stats system in envoyproxy/envoy v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple tightly integrated components:\\n\\n**Core Symbol Table (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h/.cc)**: The SymbolTable manages a compact namespace for stats using symbol interning. StatName objects represent interned stat names, while StatNamePool provides pooled allocation for groups of related stats. StatNameManagedStorage allows automatic cleanup of StatNames without explicit free() calls.\\n\\n**Stats Scope Hierarchy (envoy/stats/store.h, source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/.cc, source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/.cc)**: The Stats::Scope interface defines the hierarchy for creating statistics. ThreadLocalStoreImpl provides the main implementation with thread-local caching and scope management (ScopeImpl class), while IsolatedStoreImpl provides a simpler, non-thread-safe variant with IsolatedScopeImpl. Both implement the Stats::Scope interface for creating counters, gauges, and histograms.\\n\\n**Allocator & Metrics (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/metric_impl.h/.cc)**: AllocatorImpl creates metric objects (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, TextReadout). MetricImpl and MetricHelper manage the internal representation combining stat names, tag-extracted names, and StatNameTagVectors. Concrete implementations include CounterImpl, GaugeImpl, TextReadoutImpl, and HistogramImpl/ThreadLocalHistogramImpl/ParentHistogramImpl.\\n\\n**Tag Extraction System (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/.cc, source/common/config/well_known_names.h/.cc)**: TagProducerImpl extracts tags from metric names based on regex patterns and fixed values. Multiple TagExtractor implementations handle different extraction strategies: TagExtractorImplBase (regex-based), TagExtractorStdRegexImpl, TagExtractorRe2Impl, TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values), and TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based patterns). Well-known tag definitions are stored in well_known_names.cc.\\n\\n**Statsd Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: The common statsd implementation in statsd.h/.cc provides UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink base classes with tag format support (tag_formats.h/.cc). StatsdSinkFactory, DogStatsdSinkFactory, and GraphiteStatsdSinkFactory configure and create sink instances for different protocol variants.\\n\\n**Prometheus Formatting (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_handler.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_render.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_html_render.h/.cc)**: PrometheusStatsFormatter converts metrics to Prometheus text format with proper tag formatting. StatsHandler and related render classes handle HTTP endpoint responses. PrometheusStatsFormatter::statsAsPrometheus() is the main dispatch point for formatting counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts.\\n\\n**Additional Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: Metrics service sink for gRPC, OpenTelemetry/OTLP sink implementation with OtlpMetricsFlusherImpl, Hystrix sink, and WebAssembly-based sinks. Each sink factory extends the configuration pattern to support different output formats.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**: utility.h/.cc provides helpers for scope/stat creation, histogram_impl.h/.cc implements histogram bucketing, tag_utility.h/.cc handles tag joining with stat names, stats_matcher_impl.h/.cc filters which stats are created, stat_merger.h/.cc merges stats across hot restarts, and deferred_creation.h allows lazy stat initialization.\\n\\n**Public APIs (envoy/stats/)**: Headers define the public interfaces for Scope, Store, StoreRoot, Sink, Histogram, Allocator, TagProducer, and SymbolTable. stats_macros.h provides convenience macros for stat definition. custom_stat_namespaces.h supports custom metrics outside the core Envoy stats.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":8593,"cache_read_input_tokens":82555,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":8593},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9029939b-44d2-4521-b26e-aafe5fd28a11","uuid":"82c851da-3fe9-4206-8ee0-3708b1d020f6"}

\"text\": \"The Envoy Stats system in envoyproxy/envoy v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple tightly integrated components:\\n\\n**Core Symbol Table (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h/.cc)**: The SymbolTable manages a compact namespace for stats using symbol interning. StatName objects represent interned stat names, while StatNamePool provides pooled allocation for groups of related stats. StatNameManagedStorage allows automatic cleanup of StatNames without explicit free() calls.\\n\\n**Stats Scope Hierarchy (envoy/stats/store.h, source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/.cc, source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/.cc)**: The Stats::Scope interface defines the hierarchy for creating statistics. ThreadLocalStoreImpl provides the main implementation with thread-local caching and scope management (ScopeImpl class), while IsolatedStoreImpl provides a simpler, non-thread-safe variant with IsolatedScopeImpl. Both implement the Stats::Scope interface for creating counters, gauges, and histograms.\\n\\n**Allocator & Metrics (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/metric_impl.h/.cc)**: AllocatorImpl creates metric objects (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, TextReadout). MetricImpl and MetricHelper manage the internal representation combining stat names, tag-extracted names, and StatNameTagVectors. Concrete implementations include CounterImpl, GaugeImpl, TextReadoutImpl, and HistogramImpl/ThreadLocalHistogramImpl/ParentHistogramImpl.\\n\\n**Tag Extraction System (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/.cc, source/common/config/well_known_names.h/.cc)**: TagProducerImpl extracts tags from metric names based on regex patterns and fixed values. Multiple TagExtractor implementations handle different extraction strategies: TagExtractorImplBase (regex-based), TagExtractorStdRegexImpl, TagExtractorRe2Impl, TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values), and TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based patterns). Well-known tag definitions are stored in well_known_names.cc.\\n\\n**Statsd Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: The common statsd implementation in statsd.h/.cc provides UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink base classes with tag format support (tag_formats.h/.cc). StatsdSinkFactory, DogStatsdSinkFactory, and GraphiteStatsdSinkFactory configure and create sink instances for different protocol variants.\\n\\n**Prometheus Formatting (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_handler.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_render.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_html_render.h/.cc)**: PrometheusStatsFormatter converts metrics to Prometheus text format with proper tag formatting. StatsHandler and related render classes handle HTTP endpoint responses. PrometheusStatsFormatter::statsAsPrometheus() is the main dispatch point for formatting counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts.\\n\\n**Additional Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: Metrics service sink for gRPC, OpenTelemetry/OTLP sink implementation with OtlpMetricsFlusherImpl, Hystrix sink, and WebAssembly-based sinks. Each sink factory extends the configuration pattern to support different output formats.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**: utility.h/.cc provides helpers for scope/stat creation, histogram_impl.h/.cc implements histogram bucketing, tag_utility.h/.cc handles tag joining with stat names, stats_matcher_impl.h/.cc filters which stats are created, stat_merger.h/.cc merges stats across hot restarts, and deferred_creation.h allows lazy stat initialization.\\n\\n**Public APIs (envoy/stats/)**: Headers define the public interfaces for Scope, Store, StoreRoot, Sink, Histogram, Allocator, TagProducer, and SymbolTable. stats_macros.h provides convenience macros for stat definition. custom_stat_namespaces.h supports custom metrics outside the core Envoy stats.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
